==== De oratore 3 ====
=== LIBER TERTIVS ===
= § 1 =
(4) Instituenti(Prä)(Akt)(D) mihi(Pr)(D), Quinte(V) frater(V), eum(Pr)(A) sermonem(A) referre(Inf)(Akt) et(Kon) mandare(Inf)(Akt) huic(Pr)(D)

= § 2 =
(11) Ut(Kon) enim(Pt) Romam(A) rediit(Per)(Akt) extremo(Adj)(Abl) ludorum(G) scaenicorum(G) die(Abl), vehementer(Adv) commotus(Per)(Pas)(N)

= § 3 =
